msg:Overall, Hyatt offers a wonderful stay, there are few disappointments. The room, property design and fittings are excellent, the best and most thoughtfully designed breakfast I think I've ever had and very noticeably the friendly, helpful and facilitative stage who can't do enough for you. 

An honorable mention to staff members Kerwin, Michael the concierge and Audrey and Sia, all who couldn't do enough for a customer, made you feel welcome and taken care of, in a discreet and thoughtful way. 

There were two things I wasn't so fond of. I was relieved to know I'd booked a non-smoking room. The first room I tried smelled of cigar smoke. Michael the concierge helped me try another, on another floor. It too had background cigarette smell in the room which I had to breathe all night. As a non-smoker it wasn't very nice with every breathe I took. Such are shared air- conditioning ducts I suppose. 

Anyway I wasn't gong to try a third room. Next time I'd try for a terrace room with an outside door. The smoke would need something that would have me thinking twice whether to book again. You could smell it sometimes when walking in the corridor. 

Lastly,  the refund. Please know you'll be charged approximately another room fee as deposit. At checkout I'd forgotten to ask about its return but was later in the day informed it would need returned in 3 to 5 days. I feel this is a little bit unreasonably excessive. 

Thank you

Even if I temporarily return to the imperial capital, I am willing to stay in a hotel instead of going home to make trouble.

‚òòÔ∏èThe first choice hotel is Wangjing Hyatt.
Not only is the Hyatt close to home, convenient for staying and entertaining friends, but I also like the feeling of the Wangjing Hyatt as a breathable urban oasis. Of course, I particularly appreciate the warm and jade-like temperament and empathic closeness of the hotel staff.

‚òòÔ∏èThe hotel conditions, including catering standards, have been shared on Ctrip and other platforms before, so I won‚Äôt go into details here. This article just wants to record the hotel staff I came into contact with and express my gratitude to them.

‚òòÔ∏è I have stayed at the Park Hyatt, Grand Hyatt, and Hyatt Collection under the Hyatt Group. I have stayed at the Hyatt in Wangjing N times. This time I stayed for five days and four nights and stayed in rooms 0510 and 0855. The former has a king bed with a view. room, the latter Hyatt Suite.

‚òòÔ∏èThe landscape king bed room is facing Wangjing SOHO. Zaha Hadid's architectural language is full and round, cool and stunning. The flowing curves are not only perfectly close to nature, but also allow Kengo Kuma's classic design to complement it.

‚òòÔ∏èThe Hyatt Suite is even more outstanding, taking into account privacy and sociality as well as a convenient living layout, especially suitable for business travel. The welcome fruits, soft drinks, and snacks are very warm. Among them, Hyatt‚Äôs customized Las Condes 2022 Cabernet Sauvignon dry red wine is not luxurious, but it has a rich fruity flavor, moderate acidity and tannins. Even if you don‚Äôt know about red wine, you can You can also feel the full sincerity of the phrase "Have a very charming stay" in the welcome message in the room.

‚òòÔ∏èSincerity is ultimately reflected by people, that is, employees.
üå∫Sister Weng Ling from the housekeeping depar**ent has a gentle demeanor, a sunny attitude, decent language, and a spring breeze on her face. She pays special attention to details. She can always put herself in the shoes of the guests and nags me over and over again, such as adding more bath towels and putting more tea bags and bottles. Shui et al. never get bored or slack at all, and can be called a role model for house sisters.

üå∫Concierge Zhao Liucheng. I came in and out frequently during my stay for a few days and I met him almost every time. The young man was energetic and handsome. He never forgot to say hello to me every time. I never saw him idle for a moment, and he actively helped me. I scanned documents, packaged and sent the express efficiently, I was so touched!

üå∫Hao Ziyu at the front desk seems to have a connection with me. He handles check-in, room renewal, and check-out all by himself. He can also patiently introduce the service features of the hotel, including the difference between booking breakfast online and purchasing breakfast at the hotel front desk. The young man is very humble. . His colleague Gao Jingnan at the front desk is also very high-quality.

üî•Friends who have been to the Hyatt Hotel know that there are two restaurants on the left and right sides of the lobby, Zangyue on the south side and Xunba on the north side, which are like Suzaku and Xuanwu guarding the Market Caf√© in the center. The sunken design of the cafe is like a cornucopia, with the purple energy coming from the east passing through the lush bamboo forest covering the restaurant. I haven‚Äôt verified whether this layout has Feng Shui requirements, but during breakfast in the cafe, I had a conversation with a manager Wang Yan who came to help temporarily. After several interactions, Wang Yan‚Äôs confidence, self-motivation, and pride infected me.

‚òòÔ∏èMarket Caf√© has been reviewed in a special article before.

üå∫ Compared to coffee shops, the service and products of Zangyue Chinese Restaurant are relatively average. The Shunba Izakaya, which corresponds to Zangyue, is worth experiencing.
